ONBOARD\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <!-- Main Container -->\n    <div class="main-container">\n        <!-- State Tree Sidebar -->\n        <div class="state-tree">\n            <h3>STATE EVOLUTION TREE</h3>\n            <div id="state-tree-content"></div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Terminal Container -->\n        <div class="terminal-container">\n            <div class="terminal" id="terminal"></div>\n            <div class="input-area">\n                <input type="text" id="command-input" placeholder="murphy> enter command (type \'help\' for commands)" />\n                <button onclick="executeCommand()">EXECUTE</button>\n                <button onclick="initializeSystem()">INITIALIZE</button>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Right Sidebar -->\n        <div class="right-sidebar">\n            <!-- Phase Indicator -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>MFGC PHASES</h4>\n                <div class="phase-indicator" id="phase-indicator"></div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Metrics -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>SYSTEM METRICS</h4>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>States Generated:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-states">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>Artifacts Created:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-artifacts">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>Gates Active:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-gates">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>Confidence:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-confidence">0.00</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>Murphy Index:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-murphy">0.00</span>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Active Swarms -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>ACTIVE SWARMS</h4>\n                <div id="swarms-list"></div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Artifacts -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>GENERATED ARTIFACTS</h4>\n                <div id="artifacts-list"></div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Active Gates -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>ACTIVE GATES</h4>\n                <div id="gates-list"></div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Constraints -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>CONSTRAINTS</h4>\n                <div id="constraints-list"></div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <!-- Modal for State Details -->\n    <div class="modal" id="state-modal">\n        <div class="modal-content">\n            <span class="close-modal" onclick="closeModal()">&times;</span>\n            <h2 id="modal-title">State Details</h2>\n            <div id="modal-body"></div>\n            <div class="modal-actions">\n                <button class="modal-btn" onclick="evolveState()">EVOLVE STATE</button>\n                <button class="modal-btn" onclick="regenerateState()">REGENERATE</button>\n                <button class="modal-btn secondary" onclick="rollbackState()">ROLLBACK</button>\n                <button class="modal-btn secondary" onclick="closeModal()">CLOSE</button>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <script>\n        // ===== MURPHY SYSTEM BACKEND INTEGRATION =====\n        \n        // Phase definitions from mfgc_core.py\n        const PHASES = {\n            EXPAND: { name: \'EXPAND\', threshold: 0.3, weights: [0.9, 0.1] },\n            TYPE: { name: \'TYPE\', threshold: 0.5, weights: [0.8, 0.2] },\n            ENUMERATE: { name: \'ENUMERATE\', threshold: 0.6, weights: [0.7, 0.3] },\n            CONSTRAIN: { name: \'CONSTRAIN\', threshold: 0.65, weights: [0.5, 0.5] },\n            COLLAPSE: { name: \'COLLAPSE\', threshold: 0.7, weights: [0.3, 0.7] },\n            BIND: { name: \'BIND\', threshold: 0.75, weights: [0.2, 0.8] },\n            EXECUTE: { name: \'EXECUTE\', threshold: 0.85, weights: [0.1, 0.9] }\n        };\n\n        // Swarm types from advanced_swarm_system.py\n        const SWARM_TYPES = {\n            CREATIVE: \'creative\',\n            ANALYTICAL: \'analytical\',\n            HYBRID: \'hybrid\',\n            ADVERSARIAL: \'adversarial\',\n            SYNTHESIS: \'synthesis\',\n            OPTIMIZATION: \'optimization\'\n        };\n\n        // Constraint types from constraint_system.py\n        const CONSTRAINT_TYPES = {\n            BUDGET: \'budget\',\n            REGULATORY: \'regulatory\',\n            ARCHITECTURAL: \'architectural\',\n            PERFORMANCE: \'performance\',\n            SECURITY: \'security\',\n            TIME: \'time\',\n            RESOURCE: \'resource\',\n            BUSINESS: \'business\'\n        };\n\n        // Gate library from gate_builder.py\n        const GATE_LIBRARY = {\n            data_loss: { name: \'Data Loss Prevention\', severity: 0.8 },\n            security_breach: { name: \'Security Gate\', severity: 0.9 },\n            invalid_input: { name: \'Input Validation\', severity: 0.7 },\n            system_overload: { name: \'Load Balancing\', severity: 0.6 },\n            data_corruption: { name: \'Data Integrity\', severity: 0.8 },\n            unauthorized_action: { name: \'Authorization\', severity: 0.9 },\n            performance_degradation: { name: \'Performance\', severity: 0.5 },\n            compliance_violation: { name: \'Compliance\', severity: 0.9 },\n            resource_exhaustion: { name: \'Resource\', severity: 0.7 },\n            dependency_failure: { name: \'Dependency\', severity: 0.6 }\n        };\n\n        // System State\n        let systemState = {\n            initialized: false,\n            currentPhase: \'EXPAND\',\n            confidence: 0.0,\n            murphyIndex: 0.0,\n            states: [],\n            artifacts: [],\n            gates: [],\n            swarms: [],\n            constraints: [],\n            llms: {\n                groq: false,\n                aristotle: false,\n                onboard: false\n            },\n            selectedState: null,\n            stateCounter: 0,\n            artifactCounter: 0\n        };\n\n        // Initialize phase indicator\n        function initPhaseIndicator() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'phase-indicator\');\n            Object.keys(PHASES).forEach(phase => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'phase-step\';\n                div.id = `phase-${phase}`;\n                div.textContent = phase.substring(0, 3);\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Update phase indicator\n        function updatePhaseIndicator() {\n            Object.keys(PHASES).forEach(phase => {\n                const elem = document.getElementById(`phase-${phase}`);\n                if (phase === systemState.currentPhase) {\n                    elem.className = \'phase-step active\';\n                } else if (Object.keys(PHASES).indexOf(phase) < Object.keys(PHASES).indexOf(systemState.currentPhase)) {\n                    elem.className = \'phase-step complete\';\n                } else {\n                    elem.className = \'phase-step\';\n                }\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Terminal output\n        function terminalOutput(tag, message) {\n            const terminal = document.getElementById(\'terminal\');\n            const line = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            line.className = \'terminal-line\';\n            \n            const tagSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n            tagSpan.className = `tag tag-${tag}`;\n            tagSpan.textContent = tag.toUpperCase();\n            \n            line.appendChild(tagSpan);\n            line.appendChild(document.createTextNode(message));\n            \n            terminal.appendChild(line);\n            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;\n        }\n\n        // Toggle LLM\n        function toggleLLM(llm) {\n            systemState.llms[llm] = !systemState.llms[llm];\n            const elem = document.getElementById(`llm-${llm}`);\n            \n            if (systemState.llms[llm]) {\n                elem.className = \'llm-indicator active\';\n                terminalOutput(\'llm\', `${llm.toUpperCase()} activated - ready for inference`);\n            } else {\n                elem.className = \'llm-indicator inactive\';\n                terminalOutput(\'llm\', `${llm.toUpperCase()} deactivated`);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Create state\n        function createState(name, description, parentId = null, swarmType = null) {\n            const state = {\n                id: `STATE-${systemState.stateCounter++}`,\n                name: name,\n                description: description,\n                parentId: parentId,\n                children: [],\n                confidence: Math.random() * 0.3 + 0.5,\n                swarmType: swarmType || SWARM_TYPES.HYBRID,\n                phase: systemState.currentPhase,\n                artifacts: [],\n                gates: [],\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.states.push(state);\n            \n            if (parentId) {\n                const parent = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === parentId);\n                if (parent) {\n                    parent.children.push(state.id);\n                }\n            }\n            \n            updateMetrics();\n            renderStateTree();\n            \n            return state;\n        }\n\n        // Create artifact\n        function createArtifact(name, type, stateId, content) {\n            const artifact = {\n                id: `ARTIFACT-${systemState.artifactCounter++}`,\n                name: name,\n                type: type,\n                stateId: stateId,\n                content: content,\n                confidence: Math.random() * 0.2 + 0.7,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.artifacts.push(artifact);\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === stateId);\n            if (state) {\n                state.artifacts.push(artifact.id);\n            }\n            \n            updateMetrics();\n            renderArtifacts();\n            \n            return artifact;\n        }\n\n        // Create gate\n        function createGate(gateKey, stateId) {\n            const gateTemplate = GATE_LIBRARY[gateKey];\n            const gate = {\n                id: `GATE-${systemState.gates.length}`,\n                key: gateKey,\n                name: gateTemplate.name,\n                severity: gateTemplate.severity,\n                stateId: stateId,\n                active: true,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.gates.push(gate);\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === stateId);\n            if (state) {\n                state.gates.push(gate.id);\n            }\n            \n            updateMetrics();\n            renderGates();\n            \n            return gate;\n        }\n\n        // Create swarm\n        function createSwarm(type, stateId, purpose) {\n            const swarm = {\n                id: `SWARM-${systemState.swarms.length}`,\n                type: type,\n                stateId: stateId,\n                purpose: purpose,\n                progress: 0,\n                active: true,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.swarms.push(swarm);\n            renderSwarms();\n            \n            // Simulate swarm progress\n            const interval = setInterval(() => {\n                swarm.progress += Math.random() * 20;\n                if (swarm.progress >= 100) {\n                    swarm.progress = 100;\n                    swarm.active = false;\n                    clearInterval(interval);\n                    terminalOutput(\'swarm\', `${type.toUpperCase()} swarm completed for ${stateId}`);\n                    \n                    // Generate artifact when swarm completes\n                    const artifact = createArtifact(\n                        `${type} Analysis`,\n                        \'analysis\',\n                        stateId,\n                        `Generated by ${type} swarm`\n                    );\n                    terminalOutput(\'artifact\', `Created ${artifact.id}: ${artifact.name}`);\n                }\n                renderSwarms();\n            }, 1000);\n            \n            return swarm;\n        }\n\n        // Create constraint\n        function createConstraint(type, name, value) {\n            const constraint = {\n                id: `CONSTRAINT-${systemState.constraints.length}`,\n                type: type,\n                name: name,\n                value: value,\n                active: true,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.constraints.push(constraint);\n            renderConstraints();\n            \n            return constraint;\n        }\n\n        // Advance phase\n        function advancePhase() {\n            const phases = Object.keys(PHASES);\n            const currentIndex = phases.indexOf(systemState.currentPhase);\n            \n            if (currentIndex < phases.length - 1) {\n                const nextPhase = phases[currentIndex + 1];\n                const threshold = PHASES[nextPhase].threshold;\n                \n                if (systemState.confidence >= threshold) {\n                    systemState.currentPhase = nextPhase;\n                    terminalOutput(\'phase\', `Advanced to ${nextPhase} phase (confidence: ${systemState.confidence.toFixed(2)})`);\n                    updatePhaseIndicator();\n                    return true;\n                } else {\n                    terminalOutput(\'phase\', `Cannot advance to ${nextPhase} - confidence ${systemState.confidence.toFixed(2)} < ${threshold}`);\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        // Update metrics\n        function updateMetrics() {\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-states\').textContent = systemState.states.length;\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-artifacts\').textContent = systemState.artifacts.length;\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-gates\').textContent = systemState.gates.filter(g => g.active).length;\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-confidence\').textContent = systemState.confidence.toFixed(2);\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-murphy\').textContent = systemState.murphyIndex.toFixed(2);\n        }\n\n        // Render state tree\n        function renderStateTree() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'state-tree-content\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            const rootStates = systemState.states.filter(s => !s.parentId);\n            \n            rootStates.forEach(state => {\n                renderStateNode(state, container, 0);\n            });\n        }\n\n        function renderStateNode(state, container, depth) {\n            const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            div.className = `state-node ${depth === 1 ? \'child\' : depth === 2 ? \'grandchild\' : \'\'}`;\n            div.onclick = () => showStateModal(state.id);\n            \n            div.innerHTML = `\n                <div>${state.id}: ${state.name}</div>\n                <div class="state-confidence">Confidence: ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)} | ${state.swarmType}</div>\n            `;\n            \n            container.appendChild(div);\n            \n            // Render children\n            state.children.forEach(childId => {\n                const child = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === childId);\n                if (child) {\n                    renderStateNode(child, container, depth + 1);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render swarms\n        function renderSwarms() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'swarms-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            const activeSwarms = systemState.swarms.filter(s => s.active);\n            \n            if (activeSwarms.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No active swarms</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            activeSwarms.forEach(swarm => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = `swarm-item swarm-${swarm.type}`;\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${swarm.type.toUpperCase()}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">${swarm.purpose}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; margin-top: 3px;">Progress: ${swarm.progress.toFixed(0)}%</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render artifacts\n        function renderArtifacts() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'artifacts-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            if (systemState.artifacts.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No artifacts yet</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            systemState.artifacts.slice(-5).reverse().forEach(artifact => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'artifact-item\';\n                div.onclick = () => showArtifactModal(artifact.id);\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${artifact.id}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">${artifact.name}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; margin-top: 3px;">Confidence: ${artifact.confidence.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render gates\n        function renderGates() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'gates-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            const activeGates = systemState.gates.filter(g => g.active);\n            \n            if (activeGates.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No active gates</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            activeGates.forEach(gate => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'gate-item\';\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${gate.name}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">Severity: ${gate.severity.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render constraints\n        function renderConstraints() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'constraints-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            if (systemState.constraints.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No constraints</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            systemState.constraints.forEach(constraint => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'gate-item\';\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${constraint.name}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">${constraint.type}: ${constraint.value}</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Show state modal\n        function showStateModal(stateId) {\n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === stateId);\n            if (!state) return;\n            \n            systemState.selectedState = stateId;\n            \n            const modal = document.getElementById(\'state-modal\');\n            const title = document.getElementById(\'modal-title\');\n            const body = document.getElementById(\'modal-body\');\n            \n            title.textContent = `${state.id}: ${state.name}`;\n            \n            body.innerHTML = `\n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>State Information</h3>\n                    <div><strong>Description:</strong> ${state.description}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Phase:</strong> ${state.phase}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Confidence:</strong> ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Swarm Type:</strong> ${state.swarmType}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Created:</strong> ${new Date(state.timestamp).toLocaleString()}</div>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>Artifacts (${state.artifacts.length})</h3>\n                    ${state.artifacts.length > 0 ? state.artifacts.map(aid => {\n                        const artifact = systemState.artifacts.find(a => a.id === aid);\n                        return `<div>• ${artifact.name} (${artifact.confidence.toFixed(2)})</div>`;\n                    }).join(\'\') : \'<div>No artifacts yet</div>\'}\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>Gates (${state.gates.length})</h3>\n                    ${state.gates.length > 0 ? state.gates.map(gid => {\n                        const gate = systemState.gates.find(g => g.id === gid);\n                        return `<div>• ${gate.name} (severity: ${gate.severity.toFixed(2)})</div>`;\n                    }).join(\'\') : \'<div>No gates yet</div>\'}\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>Children (${state.children.length})</h3>\n                    ${state.children.length > 0 ? state.children.map(cid => {\n                        const child = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === cid);\n                        return `<div>• ${child.id}: ${child.name}</div>`;\n                    }).join(\'\') : \'<div>No children yet</div>\'}\n                </div>\n            `;\n            \n            modal.className = \'modal active\';\n        }\n\n        // Close modal\n        function closeModal() {\n            document.getElementById(\'state-modal\').className = \'modal\';\n            systemState.selectedState = null;\n        }\n\n        // Evolve state\n        function evolveState() {\n            if (!systemState.selectedState) return;\n            \n            const parent = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === systemState.selectedState);\n            if (!parent) return;\n            \n            // Create child state\n            const childState = createState(\n                `Evolution of ${parent.name}`,\n                `Evolved from ${parent.id} with enhanced capabilities`,\n                parent.id,\n                SWARM_TYPES.HYBRID\n            );\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `Evolved ${parent.id} → ${childState.id}`);\n            \n            // Create swarm for new state\n            createSwarm(SWARM_TYPES.HYBRID, childState.id, \'Analyze evolved state\');\n            \n            // Create gate for new state\n            createGate(\'invalid_input\', childState.id);\n            \n            closeModal();\n        }\n\n        // Regenerate state\n        function regenerateState() {\n            if (!systemState.selectedState) return;\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === systemState.selectedState);\n            if (!state) return;\n            \n            // Update confidence\n            state.confidence = Math.random() * 0.3 + 0.6;\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `Regenerated ${state.id} with new confidence: ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)}`);\n            \n            // Create new swarm\n            createSwarm(SWARM_TYPES.CREATIVE, state.id, \'Regenerate with creative approach\');\n            \n            closeModal();\n            renderStateTree();\n        }\n\n        // Rollback state\n        function rollbackState() {\n            if (!systemState.selectedState) return;\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === systemState.selectedState);\n            if (!state || !state.parentId) {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'Cannot rollback - no parent state\');\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            const parent = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === state.parentId);\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `Rolled back ${state.id} → ${parent.id}`);\n            \n            closeModal();\n            showStateModal(parent.id);\n        }\n\n        // Execute command\n        function executeCommand() {\n            const input = document.getElementById(\'command-input\');\n            const command = input.value.trim().toLowerCase();\n            input.value = \'\';\n            \n            if (!command) return;\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `murphy> ${command}`);\n            \n            if (command === \'help\') {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'Available commands:\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  help - Show this help\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  status - Show system status\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  evolve <state-id> - Evolve a state\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  regenerate <state-id> - Regenerate a state\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  advance - Advance to next phase\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  create-constraint <type> <name> <value> - Create constraint\');\n            } else if (command === \'status\') {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Phase: ${systemState.currentPhase}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Confidence: ${systemState.confidence.toFixed(2)}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `States: ${systemState.states.length}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Artifacts: ${systemState.artifacts.length}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Active Gates: ${systemState.gates.filter(g => g.active).length}`);\n            } else if (command === \'advance\') {\n                advancePhase();\n            } else if (command.startsWith(\'evolve \')) {\n                const stateId = command.split(\' \')[1];\n                systemState.selectedState = stateId;\n                evolveState();\n            } else if (command.startsWith(\'regenerate \')) {\n                const stateId = command.split(\' \')[1];\n                systemState.selectedState = stateId;\n                regenerateState();\n            } else if (command.startsWith(\'create-constraint \')) {\n                const parts = command.split(\' \');\n                if (parts.length >= 4) {\n                    const type = parts[1];\n                    const name = parts[2];\n                    const value = parts.slice(3).join(\' \');\n                    createConstraint(type, name, value);\n                    terminalOutput(\'constraint\', `Created ${type} constraint: ${name} = ${value}`);\n                }\n            } else {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Unknown command: ${command}`);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Initialize system\n        function initializeSystem() {\n            if (systemState.initialized) {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'System already initialized\');\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', \'=== MURPHY SYSTEM INITIALIZATION ===\');\n            terminalOutput(\'system\', \'Backend integration: ACTIVE\');\n            terminalOutput(\'system\', \'Loading MFGC core...\');\n            \n            // Activate LLMs\n            setTimeout(() => {\n                toggleLLM(\'groq\');\n                setTimeout(() => {\n                    toggleLLM(\'aristotle\');\n                    setTimeout(() => {\n                        toggleLLM(\'onboard\');\n                        \n                        // Create root state\n                        setTimeout(() => {\n                            terminalOutput(\'system\', \'Creating root state...\');\n                            const root = createState(\n                                \'System Initialization\',\n                                \'Root state for Murphy System runtime\',\n                                null,\n                                SWARM_TYPES.ANALYTICAL\n                            );\n                            \n                            // Create initial constraints\n                            createConstraint(CONSTRAINT_TYPES.BUDGET, \'Project Budget\', \'$100,000\');\n                            createConstraint(CONSTRAINT_TYPES.TIME, \'Timeline\', \'6 months\');\n                            createConstraint(CONSTRAINT_TYPES.SECURITY, \'Security Level\', \'High\');\n                            \n                            terminalOutput(\'constraint\', \'Loaded 3 initial constraints\');\n                            \n                            // Create initial gates\n User clicks "STATE-0" in state tree\n   ↓\n2. Frontend: showStateModal(\'STATE-0\')\n   ↓\n3. Frontend: Finds state in local cache\n   ↓\n4. Frontend: Opens modal with state details\n   ↓\n5. User clicks "EVOLVE STATE"\n   ↓\n6. Frontend: POST /api/states/STATE-0/evolve\n   ↓\n7. Backend: runtime.create_state(name, desc, parent_id=\'STATE-0\')\n   ↓\n8. Backend: Creates child state with new ID\n   ↓\n9. Backend: runtime.create_swarm(type, child_id, purpose)\n   ↓\n10. Backend: runtime.create_gate(gate_key, child_id)\n    ↓\n11. Backend: socketio.emit(\'state_created\', child_state)\n    ↓\n12. Frontend: Receives WebSocket event\n    ↓\n13. Frontend: Updates state tree with new child\n    ↓\n14. Frontend: Shows terminal output\n    ↓\n15. Backend: Starts swarm progress simulation\n    ↓\n16. Backend: socketio.emit(\'swarm_progress\', swarm)\n    ↓\n17. Frontend: Updates swarm progress bar\n    ↓\n18. Backend: Swarm reaches 100%\n    ↓\n19. Backend: runtime.create_artifact(name, type, state_id)\n    ↓\n20. Backend: socketio.emit(\'artifact_created\', artifact)\n    ↓\n21. Frontend: Adds artifact to sidebar\n    ↓\n22. Frontend: Shows terminal output\n```\n\n### Example 2: Toggling an LLM\n```\n1. User clicks "GROQ" indicator\n   ↓\n2. Frontend: toggleLLM(\'groq\')\n   ↓\n3. Frontend: POST /api/llm/groq/toggle\n   ↓\n4. Backend: runtime.toggle_llm(\'groq\')\n   ↓\n5. Backend: Toggles llms[\'groq\'][\'active\']\n   ↓\n6. Backend: If activating, initializes provider\n   ↓\n7. Backend: Returns {llm: \'groq\', active: true}\n   ↓\n8. Frontend: Updates indicator class to \'active\'\n   ↓\n9. Frontend: Shows green glow and color change\n   ↓\n10. Frontend: Shows terminal output\n```\n\n### Example 3: Advancing Phase\n```\n1. User types "advance" command\n   ↓\n2. Frontend: executeCommand()\n   ↓\n3. Frontend: POST /api/phase/advance\n   ↓\n4. Backend: runtime.advance_phase()\n   ↓\n5. Backend: Gets current phase from mfgc_state.p_t\n   ↓\n6. Backend: Gets current confidence from mfgc_state.c_t\n   ↓\n7. Backend: Checks confidence >= phase.confidence_threshold\n   ↓\n8. color: #0a0e27;\n            font-weight: bold;\n        }\n\n        .phase-step.complete {\n            background: #00cc33;\n            color: #0a0e27;\n        }\n\n        /* Scrollbar */\n        ::-webkit-scrollbar {\n            width: 8px;\n        }\n\n        ::-webkit-scrollbar-track {\n            background: #0a0e27;\n        }\n\n        ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb {\n            background: #00ff41;\n            border-radius: 4px;\n        }\n    </style>\n</head>\n<body>\n    <!-- Header with LLM Controls -->\n    <div class="header">\n        <h1>MURPHY SYSTEM - BACKEND         <div class="llm-indicator inactive" id="llm-aristotle" onclick="toggleLLM(\'aristotle\')">\n                ARISTOTLE\n            </div>\n            <div class="llm-indicator inactive" onclick="initializeSystem()">INITIALIZE</button>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <!-- Right Sidebar -->\n        <div class="right-sidebar">\n            <!-- Phase Indicator -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>MFGC PHASES</h4>\n                <div class="phase-indicator" id="phase-indicator"></div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Metrics -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>SYSTEM METRICS</h4>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>States Generated:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-states">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>Artifacts Created:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-artifacts">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>Gates Active:</span>\n                    <span class="metric-value" id="metric-gates">0</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="metric">\n                    <span>Confidence:</span>\n                    <span <h4>ACTIVE SWARMS</h4>\n                <div id="swarms-list"></div>\n            </div>\n\n            <!-- Artifacts -->\n            <div class="sidebar-section">\n                <h4>GENERATED          <div id="constraints-list"></div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <!-- Modal for State Details -->\n    <div class="modal" id="state-modal">\n        <div class="modal-content">\n            <span class="close-modal" onclick="closeModal()">&times;</span>\n            <h2 id="modal-title">State Details</h2>\n            <div id="modal-body"></div>\n            <div class="modal-actions">\n                <button class="modal-btn" onclick="evolveState()">EVOLVE STATE</button>\n                <button class="modal-btn" onclick="regenerateState()">REGENERATE</button>\n                <button class="modal-btn secondary" onclick="rollbackState()">ROLLBACK</button>\n                <button class="modal-btn secondary" onclick="closeModal()">CLOSE</button>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <script>\n        // ===== MURPHY SYSTEM BACKEND INTEGRATION =====\n        \n        // Phase definitions from mfgc_core.py\n        const PHASES = {\n            EXPAND: { name: \'EXPAND\', threshold: 0.3, weights: [0.9, 0.1] },\n            TYPE: { name: \'TYPE\', threshold: 0.5, weights: [0.8, 0.2] },\n            ENUMERATE: { name: \'ENUMERATE\', threshold: 0.6, weights: [0.7, 0.3] },\n            CONSTRAIN: { name: \'CONSTRAIN\', threshold: 0.65, weights: [0.5, 0.5] },\n            COLLAPSE: { name: \'COLLAPSE\', threshold: 0.7, weights: [0.3, 0.7] },\n            BIND: { name: \'BIND\', threshold: 0.75, weights: [0.2, 0.8] },\n            EXECUTE: { name: \'EXECUTE\', threshold: 0.85, weights: [0.1, 0.9] }\n        };\n\n        // Swarm types from advanced_swarm_system.py\n        const SWARM_TYPES = {\n            CREATIVE: \'creative\',\n            ANALYTICAL: \'analytical\',\n            HYBRID: \'hybrid\',\n            ADVERSARIAL: \'adversarial\',\n            SYNTHESIS: \'synthesis\',\n            OPTIMIZATION: \'optimization\'\n        };\n\n        // Constraint types from constraint_system.py\n        const CONSTRAINT_TYPES = {\n            BUDGET: \'budget\',\n            REGULATORY: \'regulatory\',\n            ARCHITECTURAL: \'architectural\',\n            PERFORMANCE: \'performance\',\n            SECURITY: \'security\',\n            TIME: \'time\',\n            RESOURCE: \'resource\',\n            BUSINESS: \'business\'\n        };\n\n        // Gate library from gate_builder.py\n        const GATE_LIBRARY = {\n            data_loss: { name: \'Data Loss Prevention\', severity: 0.8 },\n            security_breach: { name: \'Security Gate\', severity: 0.9 },\n            invalid_input: { name: \'Input Validation\', severity: 0.7 },\n            system_overload: { name: \'Load Balancing\', severity: 0.6 },\n            data_corruption: { name: \'Data Integrity\', severity: 0.8 },\n            unauthorized_action: { name: \'Authorization\', severity: 0.9 },\n            performance_degradation: { name: \'Performance\', severity: 0.5 },\n            compliance_violation: { name: \'Compliance\', severity: 0.9 },\n            resource_exhaustion: { name: \'Resource\', severity: 0.7 },\n            dependency_failure: { name: \'Dependency\', severity: 0.6 }\n        };\n\n        // System State\n        let systemState = {\n            initialized: false,\n            currentPhase: \'EXPAND\',\n            confidence: 0.0,\n            murphyIndex: 0.0,\n            states: [],\n            artifacts: [],\n            gates: [],\n            swarms: [],\n            constraints: [],\n            llms: {\n                groq: false,\n                aristotle: false,\n                onboard: false\n            },\n            selectedState: null,\n            stateCounter: 0,\n            artifactCounter: 0\n        };\n\n        // Initialize phase indicator\n        function initPhaseIndicator() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'phase-indicator\');\n            Object.keys(PHASES).forEach(phase => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'phase-step\';\n                div.id = `phase-${phase}`;\n                div.textContent = phase.substring(0, 3);\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Update phase indicator\n        function updatePhaseIndicator() {\n            Object.keys(PHASES).forEach(phase => {\n                const elem = document.getElementById(`phase-${phase}`);\n                if (phase === systemState.currentPhase) {\n                    elem.className = \'phase-step active\';\n                } else if (Object.keys(PHASES).indexOf(phase) < Object.keys(PHASES).indexOf(systemState.currentPhase)) {\n                    elem.className = \'phase-step complete\';\n                } else {\n                    elem.className = \'phase-step\';\n                }\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Terminal output\n        function terminalOutput(tag, message) {\n            const terminal = document.getElementById(\'terminal\');\n            const line = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            line.className = \'terminal-line\';\n            \n            const tagSpan = document.createElement(\'span\');\n            tagSpan.className = `tag tag-${tag}`;\n            tagSpan.textContent = tag.toUpperCase();\n            \n            line.appendChild(tagSpan);\n            line.appendChild(document.createTextNode(message));\n            \n            terminal.appendChild(line);\n            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;\n        }\n\n        // Toggle LLM\n        function toggleLLM(llm) {\n            systemState.llms[llm] = !systemState.llms[llm];\n            const elem = document.getElementById(`llm-${llm}`);\n            \n            if (systemState.llms[llm]) {\n                elem.className = \'llm-indicator active\';\n                terminalOutput(\'llm\', `${llm.toUpperCase()} activated - ready for inference`);\n            } else {\n                elem.className = \'llm-indicator inactive\';\n                terminalOutput(\'llm\', `${llm.toUpperCase()} deactivated`);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Create state\n        function createState(name, description, parentId = null, swarmType = null) {\n            const state = {\n                id: `STATE-${systemState.stateCounter++}`,\n                name: name,\n                description: description,\n                parentId: parentId,\n                children: [],\n                confidence: Math.random() * 0.3 + 0.5,\n                swarmType: swarmType || SWARM_TYPES.HYBRID,\n                phase: systemState.currentPhase,\n                artifacts: [],\n                gates: [],\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.states.push(state);\n            \n            if (parentId) {\n                const parent = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === parentId);\n                if (parent) {\n                    parent.children.push(state.id);\n                }\n            }\n            \n            updateMetrics();\n            renderStateTree();\n            \n            return state;\n        }\n\n        // Create artifact\n        function createArtifact(name, type, stateId, content) {\n            const artifact = {\n                id: `ARTIFACT-${systemState.artifactCounter++}`,\n                name: name,\n                type: type,\n                stateId: stateId,\n                content: content,\n                confidence: Math.random() * 0.2 + 0.7,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.artifacts.push(artifact);\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === stateId);\n            if (state) {\n                state.artifacts.push(artifact.id);\n            }\n            \n            updateMetrics();\n            renderArtifacts();\n            \n            return artifact;\n        }\n\n        // Create gate\n        function createGate(gateKey, stateId) {\n            const gateTemplate = GATE_LIBRARY[gateKey];\n            const gate = {\n                id: `GATE-${systemState.gates.length}`,\n                key: gateKey,\n                name: gateTemplate.name,\n                severity: gateTemplate.severity,\n                stateId: stateId,\n                active: true,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.gates.push(gate);\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === stateId);\n            if (state) {\n                state.gates.push(gate.id);\n            }\n            \n            updateMetrics();\n            renderGates();\n            \n            return gate;\n        }\n\n        // Create swarm\n        function createSwarm(type, stateId, purpose) {\n            const swarm = {\n                id: `SWARM-${systemState.swarms.length}`,\n                type: type,\n                stateId: stateId,\n                purpose: purpose,\n                progress: 0,\n                active: true,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.swarms.push(swarm);\n            renderSwarms();\n            \n            // Simulate swarm progress\n            const interval = setInterval(() => {\n                swarm.progress += Math.random() * 20;\n                if (swarm.progress >= 100) {\n                    swarm.progress = 100;\n                    swarm.active = false;\n                    clearInterval(interval);\n                    terminalOutput(\'swarm\', `${type.toUpperCase()} swarm completed for ${stateId}`);\n                    \n                    // Generate artifact when swarm completes\n                    const artifact = createArtifact(\n                        `${type} Analysis`,\n                        \'analysis\',\n                        stateId,\n                        `Generated by ${type} swarm`\n                    );\n                    terminalOutput(\'artifact\', `Created ${artifact.id}: ${artifact.name}`);\n                }\n                renderSwarms();\n            }, 1000);\n            \n            return swarm;\n        }\n\n        // Create constraint\n        function createConstraint(type, name, value) {\n            const constraint = {\n                id: `CONSTRAINT-${systemState.constraints.length}`,\n                type: type,\n                name: name,\n                value: value,\n                active: true,\n                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()\n            };\n            \n            systemState.constraints.push(constraint);\n            renderConstraints();\n            \n            return constraint;\n        }\n\n        // Advance phase\n        function advancePhase() {\n            const phases = Object.keys(PHASES);\n            const currentIndex = phases.indexOf(systemState.currentPhase);\n            \n            if (currentIndex < phases.length - 1) {\n                const nextPhase = phases[currentIndex + 1];\n                const threshold = PHASES[nextPhase].threshold;\n                \n                if (systemState.confidence >= threshold) {\n                    systemState.currentPhase = nextPhase;\n                    terminalOutput(\'phase\', `Advanced to ${nextPhase} phase (confidence: ${systemState.confidence.toFixed(2)})`);\n                    updatePhaseIndicator();\n                    return true;\n                } else {\n                    terminalOutput(\'phase\', `Cannot advance to ${nextPhase} - confidence ${systemState.confidence.toFixed(2)} < ${threshold}`);\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        // Update metrics\n        function updateMetrics() {\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-states\').textContent = systemState.states.length;\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-artifacts\').textContent = systemState.artifacts.length;\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-gates\').textContent = systemState.gates.filter(g => g.active).length;\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-confidence\').textContent = systemState.confidence.toFixed(2);\n            document.getElementById(\'metric-murphy\').textContent = systemState.murphyIndex.toFixed(2);\n        }\n\n        // Render state tree\n        function renderStateTree() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'state-tree-content\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            const rootStates = systemState.states.filter(s => !s.parentId);\n            \n            rootStates.forEach(state => {\n                renderStateNode(state, container, 0);\n            });\n        }\n\n        function renderStateNode(state, container, depth) {\n            const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            div.className = `state-node ${depth === 1 ? \'child\' : depth === 2 ? \'grandchild\' : \'\'}`;\n            div.onclick = () => showStateModal(state.id);\n            \n            div.innerHTML = `\n                <div>${state.id}: ${state.name}</div>\n                <div class="state-confidence">Confidence: ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)} | ${state.swarmType}</div>\n            `;\n            \n            container.appendChild(div);\n            \n            // Render children\n            state.children.forEach(childId => {\n                const child = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === childId);\n                if (child) {\n                    renderStateNode(child, container, depth + 1);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render swarms\n        function renderSwarms() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'swarms-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            const activeSwarms = systemState.swarms.filter(s => s.active);\n            \n            if (activeSwarms.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No active swarms</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            activeSwarms.forEach(swarm => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = `swarm-item swarm-${swarm.type}`;\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${swarm.type.toUpperCase()}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">${swarm.purpose}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; margin-top: 3px;">Progress: ${swarm.progress.toFixed(0)}%</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render artifacts\n        function renderArtifacts() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'artifacts-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            if (systemState.artifacts.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No artifacts yet</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            systemState.artifacts.slice(-5).reverse().forEach(artifact => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'artifact-item\';\n                div.onclick = () => showArtifactModal(artifact.id);\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${artifact.id}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">${artifact.name}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; margin-top: 3px;">Confidence: ${artifact.confidence.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render gates\n        function renderGates() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'gates-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            const activeGates = systemState.gates.filter(g => g.active);\n            \n            if (activeGates.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No active gates</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            activeGates.forEach(gate => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'gate-item\';\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${gate.name}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">Severity: ${gate.severity.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Render constraints\n        function renderConstraints() {\n            const container = document.getElementById(\'constraints-list\');\n            container.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            if (systemState.constraints.length === 0) {\n                container.innerHTML = \'<div style="font-size: 11px; opacity: 0.5;">No constraints</div>\';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            systemState.constraints.forEach(constraint => {\n                const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                div.className = \'gate-item\';\n                div.innerHTML = `\n                    <div>${constraint.name}</div>\n                    <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.7;">${constraint.type}: ${constraint.value}</div>\n                `;\n                container.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Show state modal\n        function showStateModal(stateId) {\n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === stateId);\n            if (!state) return;\n            \n            systemState.selectedState = stateId;\n            \n            const modal = document.getElementById(\'state-modal\');\n            const title = document.getElementById(\'modal-title\');\n            const body = document.getElementById(\'modal-body\');\n            \n            title.textContent = `${state.id}: ${state.name}`;\n            \n            body.innerHTML = `\n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>State Information</h3>\n                    <div><strong>Description:</strong> ${state.description}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Phase:</strong> ${state.phase}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Confidence:</strong> ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Swarm Type:</strong> ${state.swarmType}</div>\n                    <div><strong>Created:</strong> ${new Date(state.timestamp).toLocaleString()}</div>\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>Artifacts (${state.artifacts.length})</h3>\n                    ${state.artifacts.length > 0 ? state.artifacts.map(aid => {\n                        const artifact = systemState.artifacts.find(a => a.id === aid);\n                        return `<div>\\u2022 ${artifact.name} (${artifact.confidence.toFixed(2)})</div>`;\n                    }).join(\'\') : \'<div>No artifacts yet</div>\'}\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>Gates (${state.gates.length})</h3>\n                    ${state.gates.length > 0 ? state.gates.map(gid => {\n                        const gate = systemState.gates.find(g => g.id === gid);\n                        return `<div>\\u2022 ${gate.name} (severity: ${gate.severity.toFixed(2)})</div>`;\n                    }).join(\'\') : \'<div>No gates yet</div>\'}\n                </div>\n                \n                <div class="modal-section">\n                    <h3>Children (${state.children.length})</h3>\n                    ${state.children.length > 0 ? state.children.map(cid => {\n                        const child = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === cid);\n                        return `<div>\\u2022 ${child.id}: ${child.name}</div>`;\n                    }).join(\'\') : \'<div>No children yet</div>\'}\n                </div>\n            `;\n            \n            modal.className = \'modal active\';\n        }\n\n        // Close modal\n        function closeModal() {\n            document.getElementById(\'state-modal\').className = \'modal\';\n            systemState.selectedState = null;\n        }\n\n        // Evolve state\n        function evolveState() {\n            if (!systemState.selectedState) return;\n            \n            const parent = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === systemState.selectedState);\n            if (!parent) return;\n            \n            // Create child state\n            const childState = createState(\n                `Evolution of ${parent.name}`,\n                `Evolved from ${parent.id} with enhanced capabilities`,\n                parent.id,\n                SWARM_TYPES.HYBRID\n            );\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `Evolved ${parent.id} \\u2192 ${childState.id}`);\n            \n            // Create swarm for new state\n            createSwarm(SWARM_TYPES.HYBRID, childState.id, \'Analyze evolved state\');\n            \n            // Create gate for new state\n            createGate(\'invalid_input\', childState.id);\n            \n            closeModal();\n        }\n\n        // Regenerate state\n        function regenerateState() {\n            if (!systemState.selectedState) return;\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === systemState.selectedState);\n            if (!state) return;\n            \n            // Update confidence\n            state.confidence = Math.random() * 0.3 + 0.6;\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `Regenerated ${state.id} with new confidence: ${state.confidence.toFixed(2)}`);\n            \n            // Create new swarm\n            createSwarm(SWARM_TYPES.CREATIVE, state.id, \'Regenerate with creative approach\');\n            \n            closeModal();\n            renderStateTree();\n        }\n\n        // Rollback state\n        function rollbackState() {\n            if (!systemState.selectedState) return;\n            \n            const state = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === systemState.selectedState);\n            if (!state || !state.parentId) {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'Cannot rollback - no parent state\');\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            const parent = systemState.states.find(s => s.id === state.parentId);\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `Rolled back ${state.id} \\u2192 ${parent.id}`);\n            \n            closeModal();\n            showStateModal(parent.id);\n        }\n\n        // Execute command\n        function executeCommand() {\n            const input = document.getElementById(\'command-input\');\n            const command = input.value.trim().toLowerCase();\n            input.value = \'\';\n            \n            if (!command) return;\n            \n            terminalOutput(\'system\', `murphy> ${command}`);\n            \n            if (command === \'help\') {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'Available commands:\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  help - Show this help\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  status - Show system status\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  evolve <state-id> - Evolve a state\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  regenerate <state-id> - Regenerate a state\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  advance - Advance to next phase\');\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'  create-constraint <type> <name> <value> - Create constraint\');\n            } else if (command === \'status\') {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Phase: ${systemState.currentPhase}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Confidence: ${systemState.confidence.toFixed(2)}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `States: ${systemState.states.length}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Artifacts: ${systemState.artifacts.length}`);\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Active Gates: ${systemState.gates.filter(g => g.active).length}`);\n            } else if (command === \'advance\') {\n                advancePhase();\n            } else if (command.startsWith(\'evolve \')) {\n                const stateId = command.split(\' \')[1];\n                systemState.selectedState = stateId;\n                evolveState();\n            } else if (command.startsWith(\'regenerate \')) {\n                const stateId = command.split(\' \')[1];\n                systemState.selectedState = stateId;\n                regenerateState();\n            } else if (command.startsWith(\'create-constraint \')) {\n                const parts = command.split(\' \');\n                if (parts.length >= 4) {\n                    const type = parts[1];\n                    const name = parts[2];\n                    const value = parts.slice(3).join(\' \');\n                    createConstraint(type, name, value);\n                    terminalOutput(\'constraint\', `Created ${type} constraint: ${name} = ${value}`);\n                }\n            } else {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', `Unknown command: ${command}`);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Initialize system\n        function initializeSystem() {\n            if (systemState.initialized) {\n                terminalOutput(\'system\', \'System already     messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],\n                model="mixtral-8x7b-32768",\n                temperature=0.7,\n                max_tokens=2000\n            )\n            return response.choices[0].message.content\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Groq error: {e}")\n            return await self._call_onboard(prompt)\n    \n    async def _call_anthropic(self, prompt: str) -> str:\n        """Call Anthropic API"""\n        try:\n            response = self.anthropic.messages.create(\n                model="claude-3-sonnet-20240229",\n                max_tokens=2000,\n                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}]\n            )\n            return response.content[0].text\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Anthropic error: {e}")\n            return await self._call_onboard(prompt)\n    \n    async def _call_onboard(self, prompt: str) -> str:\n        """Fallback to onboard LLM"""\n        # \n    def __init__(self, doc_id: str, title: str, content: str, doc_type: str):\n        self.doc_id = doc_id\n        self.title = title\n        self.content = content\n        self.doc_type = self.created_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n    def magnify(self, domain: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Expand domain expertise"""\n        self.domain_depth += 15\n        self.confidence += 0.1\n        self.history.append({\n            "action": "magnify",\n            "domain": domain,\n            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()\n        })\n        return self.to_dict()\n    \n    def simplify(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Distill to essentials"""\n        self.domain_depth = max(0, self.domain_depth - 10)\n        self.confidence += 0.05\n        self.history.append({\n            "action": "simplify",\n            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()\n        })\n        return self.to_dict()\n    \n    def solidify(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Solidify document for prompt generation"""\n        self.state = "SOLIDIFIED"\n        self.confidence = min(1.0, self.confidence + 0.2)\n        self.history.append({\n            "action": "solidify",\n            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()\n        })\n        return self.to_dict()\n    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        return {\n            "doc_id": self.doc_id,\n            "title": self.title,\n            "content": self.content,\n            "doc_type": self.doc_type,\n            "state": self.state,\n            "confidence": self.confidence,\n            "domain_depth": self.domain_depth,\n            "history": self.history,\n            "children": self.children,\n            "parent_id": self.parent_id,\n            "created_at": self.created_at\n        }\n\nclass MurphySystemRuntime:\n    """Complete Murphy System Runtime"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.initialized = False\n    \n        # Generate master prompt\n        master_prompt = f"""\n        Based on this document:\n        Title: {doc.title}\n        Content: {doc.content}\n        \n        Generate a prompts[domain] = await self.llm_router.route_request(domain_prompt, "generative")\n        \n        return prompts\n    \n    def assign_swarm_tasks(self, prompts: Dict[str, str]) -> List[Dict[str, "CFO",\n            "regulatory": "Compliance Officer",\n            "sales": "Sales Director",\n            "operations": "Operations Manager"\n        }\n        \n        for domain, prompt in "task_id": f"TASK-{len(tasks)}",\n                "domain": domain,\n                "role": role,\n                "prompt": prompt,\n                "status": "assigned",\n                "created_at": datetime.now().isoformat()\n            }\n            tasks.append(task)\n            \n        return tasks\n    \n    async def execute_swarm_task(self, task: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Execute a swarm task"""\n        task["status"] = "executing"\n        socketio.emit(\'task_started\', task)\n        \n        # Execute with LLM\n        result = await         const content = document.getElementById(\'content-editor\');\n            content.innerHTML = `\n                <h2>Company Information</h2>\n                <p><strong>Company systemState.documents[doc.id] = doc;\n            \n            updateDocumentDisplay();\n            addStateNode(doc.id, title, \'INITIAL\', 0.45);\n        }\n\n        // Update document display\n        function updateDocumentDisplay() {\n            const doc = systemState.currentDocument;\n            if (!doc) return;\n            \n document.getElementById(\'progress-domain\').style.width = doc.domainDepth + \'%\';\n        }\n\n        // Magnify document\n        function magnifyDocument() {\n            const doc = + 0.1);\n            doc.history.push({action: \'magnify\', timestamp: new Date().toISOString()});\n            \n            updateDocumentDisplay();\n            addStateNode(doc.id, `${doc.title} doc.history.push({action: \'simplify\', timestamp: new Date().toISOString()});\n            \n            updateDocumentDisplay();\n            addStateNode(doc.id, `${doc.title} (Simplified)`, editor.contentEditable = true;\n            editor.focus();\n        }\n\n        // Solidify document\n        function solidifyDocument() {\n            const doc = systemState.currentDocument;\n          domain: domain,\n                purpose: purpose,\n                progress: 0,\n                status: \'active\'\n            };\n            \n            systemState.swarms.push(swarm);\n            renderSwarms();\n            \n            // Simulate progress\n            const interval = setInterval(() => {\n                swarm.progress += list.appendChild(div);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Generate domain gates\n        function generateDomainGates(domain) {\n            const gateTemplates = {\n                \'Engineering\': [\'Load Calculations\', \'Code Compliance\', \'Safety Factors\'],\n                \'Financial\': [\'Budget Constraint\', \'ROI Threshold\', \'Cash Flow\'],\n
